    def assert_error_contains(
        result: CLIResult,
        *,
        field: str | None = None,
        error_type: str | None = None,
        message_contains: str | None = None,
    ) -> None:
        """Assert exit code 1 and that at least one error matches the criteria."""
        assert_error(result)
        assert result.json is not None, f"Expected JSON output, got:\n{result.stdout}"
        errors = result.json.get("errors", [])
        assert errors, "Expected at least one error"
        for err in errors:
            if field is not None and err.get("field") != field:
                continue
            if error_type is not None and err.get("type") != error_type:
                continue
            if message_contains is not None and message_contains not in err.get("message", ""):
                continue
            return  # Match found
>       assert False, (

run_cli = <function run_cli.<locals>._run at 0x740539338400>
tmp_path = PosixPath('/tmp/pytest-of-agent/pytest-0/test_create_unparseable_file_f0')
setup = 'nonexistent', test_id = 'file-not-found'

    @pytest.mark.error
    @pytest.mark.parametrize(
        "setup,test_id",
        [
            ("nonexistent", "file-not-found"),
            ("invalid-yaml", "invalid-yaml-syntax"),
            ("non-mapping", "non-mapping-yaml"),
        ],
        ids=["file-not-found", "invalid-yaml-syntax", "non-mapping-yaml"],
    )
    def test_create_unparseable_file(
        run_cli, tmp_path: Path, setup: str, test_id: str
    ) -> None:
        """mesh create with missing, unparsable, or non-mapping input yields parse error."""
        if setup == "nonexistent":
            result = run_cli(["mesh", "create", "-f", str(tmp_path / "nope.yaml")])
        elif setup == "invalid-yaml":
            bad_file = tmp_path / "bad.yaml"
            bad_file.write_text(":::invalid yaml{{{\n")
            result = run_cli(["mesh", "create", "-f", str(bad_file)])
        else:  # non-mapping
            scalar_file = tmp_path / "scalar.yaml"
            scalar_file.write_text("just a string\n")
            result = run_cli(["mesh", "create", "-f", str(scalar_file)])
    
>       assert_error_contains(result, field="", error_type="parse")

result = CLIResult(stdout='{\n  "errors": [\n    {\n      "field": "yaml",\n      "type": "invalid",\n      "message": "[Errno ...': "[Errno 2] No such file or directory: '/tmp/pytest-of-agent/pytest-0/test_create_unparseable_file_f0/nope.yaml'"}]})

    def assert_error_contains(
        result: CLIResult,
        *,
        field: str | None = None,
        error_type: str | None = None,
        message_contains: str | None = None,
    ) -> None:
        """Assert exit code 1 and that at least one error matches the criteria."""
        assert_error(result)
        assert result.json is not None, f"Expected JSON output, got:\n{result.stdout}"
        errors = result.json.get("errors", [])
        assert errors, "Expected at least one error"
        for err in errors:
            if field is not None and err.get("field") != field:
                continue
            if error_type is not None and err.get("type") != error_type:
                continue
            if message_contains is not None and message_contains not in err.get("message", ""):
                continue
            return  # Match found
>       assert False, (
            f"No error matching field={field!r}, type={error_type!r}, "
            f"message_contains={message_contains!r}.\n"
            f"Errors:\n{json.dumps(errors, indent=2)}"
        )

    def assert_error_contains(
        result: CLIResult,
        *,
        field: str | None = None,
        error_type: str | None = None,
        message_contains: str | None = None,
    ) -> None:
        """Assert exit code 1 and that at least one error matches the criteria."""
        assert_error(result)
        assert result.json is not None, f"Expected JSON output, got:\n{result.stdout}"
        errors = result.json.get("errors", [])
        assert errors, "Expected at least one error"
        for err in errors:
            if field is not None and err.get("field") != field:
                continue
            if error_type is not None and err.get("type") != error_type:
                continue
            if message_contains is not None and message_contains not in err.get("message", ""):
                continue
            return  # Match found
>       assert False, (
            f"No error matching field={field!r}, type={error_type!r}, "
            f"message_contains={message_contains!r}.\n"

        )

    def assert_error_contains(
        result: CLIResult,
        *,
        field: str | None = None,
        error_type: str | None = None,
        message_contains: str | None = None,
    ) -> None:
        """Assert exit code 1 and that at least one error matches the criteria."""
        assert_error(result)
        assert result.json is not None, f"Expected JSON output, got:\n{result.stdout}"
        errors = result.json.get("errors", [])
        assert errors, "Expected at least one error"
        for err in errors:
            if field is not None and err.get("field") != field:
                continue
            if error_type is not None and err.get("type") != error_type:
                continue
            if message_contains is not None and message_contains not in err.get("message", ""):
                continue
            return  # Match found
>       assert False, (
            f"No error matching field={field!r}, type={error_type!r}, "
            f"message_contains={message_contains!r}.\n"
            f"Errors:\n{json.dumps(errors, indent=2)}"
        )

E           }
E         ]
E       assert False

result = CLIResult(stdout='{\n  "errors": [\n    {\n      "field": "metadata.name",\n      "type": "not_found",\n      "message...eturncode=1, json={'errors': [{'field': 'metadata.name', 'type': 'not_found', 'message': "mesh 'my-mesh' not found"}]})

    def assert_error_contains(
        result: CLIResult,
        *,
        field: str | None = None,
        error_type: str | None = None,
        message_contains: str | None = None,
    ) -> None:
        """Assert exit code 1 and that at least one error matches the criteria."""
        assert_error(result)
        assert result.json is not None, f"Expected JSON output, got:\n{result.stdout}"
        errors = result.json.get("errors", [])
        assert errors, "Expected at least one error"
        for err in errors:
            if field is not None and err.get("field") != field:
                continue
            if error_type is not None and err.get("type") != error_type:
                continue
            if message_contains is not None and message_contains not in err.get("message", ""):
                continue
            return  # Match found
>       assert False, (
            f"No error matching field={field!r}, type={error_type!r}, "
            f"message_contains={message_contains!r}.\n"
            f"Errors:\n{json.dumps(errors, indent=2)}"
        )
E       AssertionError: No error matching field='spec.network.storage.size', type='immutable', message_contains=None.
E         Errors:
E         [

E             "field": "metadata.name",
E             "type": "not_found",
E             "message": "mesh 'my-mesh' not found"
E           }
E         ]
E       assert False

    @pytest.mark.functionality

    def assert_error_contains(
        result: CLIResult,
        *,
        field: str | None = None,
        error_type: str | None = None,
        message_contains: str | None = None,
    ) -> None:
        """Assert exit code 1 and that at least one error matches the criteria."""
        assert_error(result)
        assert result.json is not None, f"Expected JSON output, got:\n{result.stdout}"
        errors = result.json.get("errors", [])
        assert errors, "Expected at least one error"
        for err in errors:
            if field is not None and err.get("field") != field:
                continue
            if error_type is not None and err.get("type") != error_type:
                continue
            if message_contains is not None and message_contains not in err.get("message", ""):
                continue
            return  # Match found
>       assert False, (
            f"No error matching field={field!r}, type={error_type!r}, "
            f"message_contains={message_contains!r}.\n"
            f"Errors:\n{json.dumps(errors, indent=2)}"
        )

E           }
E         ]
